94	
95	async def get_config(
96	    host: str, token: Optional[str], semver: Optional[str] = None, config_file: Optional[str] = None
97	) -> Dict[str, Any]:
98	    if host:
99	        host = host.rstrip("/")
100	
101	    config = {}
102	    try:
103	        async with aiofiles.open(config_file or Path(getcwd()) / ".tinyb") as file:
104	            res = await file.read()
105	            config = json.loads(res)
106	    except OSError:
107	        pass
108	    except json.decoder.JSONDecodeError:
109	        click.echo(FeedbackManager.error_load_file_config(config_file=config_file))
110	        return config
111	
112	    config["token_passed"] = token
113	    config["token"] = token or config.get("token", None)
114	    config["semver"] = semver or config.get("semver", None)
115	    config["host"] = host or config.get("host", DEFAULT_API_HOST)
116	    config["workspaces"] = config.get("workspaces", [])

95	async def get_config(
96	    host: str, token: Optional[str], semver: Optional[str] = None, config_file: Optional[str] = None
97	) -> Dict[str, Any]:
98	    if host:
99	        host = host.rstrip("/")
100	
101	    config = {}
102	    try:
103	        async with aiofiles.open(config_file or Path(getcwd()) / ".tinyb") as file:
104	            res = await file.read()
105	            config = json.loads(res)

95	async def get_config(
96	    host: str, token: Optional[str], semver: Optional[str] = None, config_file: Optional[str] = None
97	) -> Dict[str, Any]:
98	    if host:
99	        host = host.rstrip("/")
100	
101	    config = {}
102	    try:
103	        async with aiofiles.open(config_file or Path(getcwd()) / ".tinyb") as file:
104	            res = await file.read()
105	            config = json.loads(res)
106	    except OSError:
107	        pass
108	    except json.decoder.JSONDecodeError:
109	        click.echo(FeedbackManager.error_load_file_config(config_file=config_file))
110	        return config

96	    host: str, token: Optional[str], semver: Optional[str] = None, config_file: Optional[str] = None
97	) -> Dict[str, Any]:
98	    if host:
99	        host = host.rstrip("/")
100	
101	    config = {}
102	    try:
103	        async with aiofiles.open(config_file or Path(getcwd()) / ".tinyb") as file:
104	            res = await file.read()
105	            config = json.loads(res)
106	    except OSError:
107	        pass
108	    except json.decoder.JSONDecodeError:
109	        click.echo(FeedbackManager.error_load_file_config(config_file=config_file))
110	        return config
111	
112	    config["token_passed"] = token
113	    config["token"] = token or config.get("token", None)
114	    config["semver"] = semver or config.get("semver", None)
115	    config["host"] = host or config.get("host", DEFAULT_API_HOST)
116	    config["workspaces"] = config.get("workspaces", [])
117	    config["cwd"] = config.get("cwd", getcwd())
